about_this_resource_text: <h2 class="subhead">Description</h2><p>In this lecture,
  Prof. Gruber continues talking about factor markets by explaining how capital markets
  influence real world decisions. See <a href="./resolveuid/e4635a413517f55c518f491dae1f8f0a">Handout
  17</a> for relevant graphs for this lecture.&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Instructor:</strong>
  Prof. Jonathan Gruber</p><p>&nbsp;</p>

  <span m="1080840">before</span> <span m="1081200">or after.</span> <span m="1081920">We</span>
  <span m="1082040">had</span> <span m="1082130">very</span> <span m="1082340">rapid</span>
  <span m="1082700">inflation</span> <span m="1083720">in</span> <span m="1083870">the</span>
  <span m="1083930">1970s.</span> <span m="1085360">It</span> <span m="1085580">then</span>
  <span m="1085990">has then</span> <span m="1086480">since</span> <span m="1086780">flattened,</span>
  <span m="1087260">and</span> <span m="1087340">inflation</span> <span m="1087800">has</span>
  <span m="1087890">been</span> <span m="1088010">much</span> <span m="1088250">slower.</span>
  <span m="1088490">And</span> <span m="1088580">inflation</span> <span m="1089030">averages</span>
  <span m="1089390">about</span> <span m="1089570">3%</span> <span m="1090050">a</span>
  <span m="1090110">year.</span></p><p><span m="1091160">OK,</span> <span m="1091910">so</span>
  <span m="1092060">basically,</span> <span m="1092390">that's</span> <span m="1092630">how</span>
  <span m="1092750">we</span> <span m="1092870">measure</span> <span m="1093140">inflation.</span>
  <span m="1095545">Now,</span> <span m="1095890">the</span> <span m="1095980">question</span>
  <span m="1096490">is,</span> <span m="1097360">how</span> <span m="1097750">does</span>
  <span m="1097930">that</span> <span m="1098080">affect</span> <span m="1098500">our</span>
  <span m="1098620">thinking</span> <span m="1099550">about</span> <span m="1099820">present</span>
  <span m="1100180">value</span> <span m="1101230">if</span> <span m="1101410">there's</span>
  <span m="1101590">actually</span> <span m="1101920">inflation?</span> <span m="1103210">And</span>
  <span m="1103300">the</span> <span m="1103390">bottom</span> <span m="1103720">line</span>
  <span m="1104080">is,</span> <span m="1105040">we</span> <span m="1105220">don't</span>
  <span m="1105580">care</span> <span m="1105940">about</span> <span m="1106240">dollars.</span>
  <span m="1107260">We</span> <span m="1107440">care</span> <span m="1107650">about</span>
  <span m="1107830">how</span> <span m="1107950">many</span> <span m="1108160">goods</span>
  <span m="1108520">we</span> <span m="1108670">can</span> <span m="1108850">buy.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="1114000">money</span> <span m="1114300">we</span> <span m="1114450">have.</span>
  <span m="1115820">It</span> <span m="1115910">matters</span> <span m="1116300">what's</span>
  <span m="1116450">happening</span> <span m="1116780">to</span> <span m="1116870">how</span>
  <span m="1116960">many</span> <span m="1117140">goods</span> <span m="1117380">we</span>
  <span m="1117470">can</span> <span m="1117620">buy.</span> <span m="1118400">Therefore,</span>
  <span m="1119180">what</span> <span m="1119360">we</span> <span m="1119480">care</span>
  <span m="1119720">about</span> <span m="1119900">is</span> <span m="1120050">not</span>
  <span m="1120740">what</span> <span m="1120920">we</span> <span m="1121010">call</span>
  <span m="1121280">the</span> <span m="1121400">nominal</span> <span m="1121940">interest</span>
  <span m="1122240">rate.</span> <span m="1122930">We</span> <span m="1123110">care</span>
  <span m="1123330">about</span> <span m="1123530">what</span> <span m="1123650">we

  <span m="1126380">we</span> <span m="1126440">define</span> <span m="1127310">as</span>

  <span m="1128960">what</span> <span m="1129100">we've been</span> <span m="1129230">talking</span>
  <span m="1129530">about,</span> <span m="1129710">we</span> <span m="1129800">see</span>
